template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}}$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tbb\+::internal\+::atomic\+\_\+do\+\_\+once (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{test__flow__graph_8cpp_a1c83625ec20fd09ecaf0e5b37c75f6f8}{F}} \&}]{initializer}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_a48f1c51623545bd4f58fbab2fa6091d0}{atomic}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetbb_1_1internal_ada4c143a836d8c23081ece16659831dc}{do\+\_\+once\+\_\+state}} $>$ \&}]{state}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



One-\/time initialization function 

/param initializer Pointer to function without arguments The variant that returns bool is used for cases when initialization can fail and it is OK to continue execution, but the state should be reset so that the initialization attempt was repeated the next time. /param state Shared state associated with initializer that specifies its initialization state. Must be initially set to \#uninitialized value (e.\+g. by means of default static zero initialization). 函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{initialize\_handler\_pointers()}{initialize\_handler\_pointers()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespacetbb_1_1internal_ad81b5f8ef24a819263e662348983fb5d} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tbb\+::internal\+::initialize\+\_\+handler\+\_\+pointers (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Initialize the allocation/free handler pointers. 

Caller is responsible for ensuring this routine is called exactly once. The routine attempts to dynamically link with the \doxylink{struct_t_b_b}{TBB} memory allocator. If that allocator is not found, it links to malloc and free. 函数调用图\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{ittnotify__static_8h_a61af67d9d838a9497ca5b188dabc1aa0}{void}} tbb\+::internal\+::throw\+\_\+exception\+\_\+v4 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacetbb_1_1internal_ace88c7330e7f616616785ffb001e04f9}{exception\+\_\+id}}}]{eid}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Gathers all throw operators in one place. 

Its purpose is to minimize code bloat that can be caused by throw operators scattered in multiple places, especially in templates.
